[30;1m27 | [0m[35mCrossHair works by repeatedly calling your functions with symbolic inputs.[0m
[30;1m28 | [0m[35mIt uses an [SMT solver] (a kind of theorem prover) to explore viable[0m
[30;1m29 | [0m[35mexecution paths and find counterexamples for you.[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35mThis is not a new idea; a Python approach was first described in[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35m[this paper].[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35mHowever, to my knowledge, CrossHair is the most complete implementation:[0m

[30;1m89 | [0m[35mCrossHair works by repeatedly calling your functions with symbolic inputs.[0m
[30;1m90 | [0m[35mIt uses an [SMT solver] (a kind of theorem prover) to explore viable[0m
[30;1m91 | [0m[35mexecution paths and find counterexamples for you.[0m
[30;1m92 | [0m[35mThis is not a new idea; a Python approach was first described in[0m
[30;1m93 | [0m[35m[this paper].[0m
[30;1m94 | [0m[35mHowever, to my knowledge, CrossHair is the most complete implementation:[0m
